create a platform for the exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management (cfr Terms of Reference).<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">One of the challenges for research organisations in the coming years will be to provide a welcoming, agile, inclusive and flexible working environment so that a new generation can flourish in the scientific workplace. At the same time it is a challenge to provide career opportunities for our more senior scientific staff. <\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">After the holiday period the team responsible for organising this event started brainstorming about the upcoming workshop. mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;'><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\">* fulfilling career paths alternative to the management path in research organisations<\/span><\/li><li style='color: rgb(0, 32, 96); The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">Following the HR CIRCLE first meeting in Brussels in 2015, CERN and the JRC are happy to invite you to the HR CIRCLE 2nd workshop focusing on Scientific Career Development.<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">The intention of the HR Circle Community is to create a platform for the exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management (cfr Terms of Reference).<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">One of the challenges for research organisations in the coming years will be to provide a welcoming, agile, inclusive and flexible working environment so that a new generation can flourish in the scientific workplace. At the same time it is a challenge to provide career opportunities for our more senior scientific staff. <\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">After the holiday period the team responsible for organising this event started brainstorming about the upcoming workshop. We tried to identify the purpose of the event and potential relevant topics for discussion. <\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt;\"><i><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/i><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">We would like to propose the following tentative ideas for the workshop:<\/font><\/span><\/p><ul style=\"list-style-type: disc; direction: ltr;\"><li style='color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 115%; font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;'><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\">* fulfilling career paths alternative to the management path in research organisations<\/span><\/li><li style='color: rgb(0, 32, 96); font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal;'><p style='color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 115%; font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;'><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\">* good practices in promoting and valorising (from an HR perspective) the scientific excellence in research<\/span><\/p><\/li><li style='color: rgb(0, 32, 96); font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal;'><p style='color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 115%; font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;'><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\">* international mobility opportunities for scientific researchers<\/span><\/p><\/li><li style='color: rgb(0, 32, 96); font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal;'><p style='color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 115%; font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;'><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\">* diversity and inclusion: how do you best ensure diversity through all HR practices<\/span><\/p><\/li><li style='color: rgb(0, 32, 96); font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal;'><p style='color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 115%; font-family: \"Calibri\",\"sans-serif\"; font-size: 11pt; font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1;'><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\">* empowering self-established networks as a means to achieve gender\/diversity objectives<\/span><\/p><\/li><\/ul><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style='color: rgb(0, 32, 96); line-height: 115%; font-family: \"Times New Roman\",\"serif\"; font-size: 7pt;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">We would very much welcome your input on the abovementioned topics and would like to know if any of these are important for you and hear which topic you would really like to discuss? Would it be possible for you to give a presentation on any of them? Or if you suggest any other topic can you help presenting it during the workshop?<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">We intend the workshop to be a mixture of presentations and participatory discussions.<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">&nbsp;<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">The workshop will take place on <b>14<sup><font size=\"2\">th<\/font><\/sup> (PM) and 15<sup><font size=\"2\">th<\/font><\/sup> (AM) November 2017<\/b>, and <b>CERN<\/b> has kindly offered to host it at its premises in <b>Gen\u00e8ve, Switzerland<\/b>.&nbsp; <\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">A networking dinner will be offered to the participants in the evening of 14 November,&nbsp; more details to follow.<\/font><\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 32, 96);\"><font face=\"Calibri\">Deadline for registrations for the workshop is Tuesday 31 October. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p page\";}}}s:26:\"field_welcome_message_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:509:\"<p>The HR CIRCLE is a network of HR professionals in research institutions across Europe. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p page\";}}}s:26:\"field_welcome_message_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:509:\"<p>The HR CIRCLE is a network of HR professionals in research institutions across Europe. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p page\";}}}s:26:\"field_welcome_message_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:509:\"<p>The HR CIRCLE is a network of HR professionals in research institutions across Europe. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p page\";}}}s:26:\"field_welcome_message_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:509:\"<p>The HR CIRCLE is a network of HR professionals in research institutions across Europe. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p page\";}}}s:26:\"field_welcome_message_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:509:\"<p>The HR CIRCLE is a network of HR professionals in research institutions across Europe. The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management. Our intention is to use these as tools in the development and improvement of HR policies (diversity strategies, mobility policy, forward planning etc.) in the participating organisations.<\/p>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:15:\"field_news_icon\";a:0:{}s:17:\"field_events_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_forum_icon\";a:0:{}s:18:\"field_library_icon\";a:0:{}s:16:\"field_about_page\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:2:{s:5:\"value\";s:2366:\"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p>The aim of the HR CIRCLE is to create a platform for the voluntary exchange of good practices in HR and more precisely, in the area of diversity and the related topics of scientific career development and competence management.<\/p><p>Our intention is to exchange and build on some of the topics listed below. We encourage members of this community to come up with other proposals for exchange and debate on this platform.<\/p><h2>1. Diversity and equal opportunities<\/h2><ul><li>Identification of obstacles in reaching gender balance: discuss the main factors that make gender balance difficult to achieve: from equal opportunities value and promotion to the reasons behind the glass ceiling.<\/li><li>Gender mainstreaming in HR: The impact of good recruitment and other HR practices in redressing the imbalance.<\/li><li>Mentoring\/coaching and other development plans towards management positions or towards alternative career paths in research. Share of practices and experiences of positive impact on valorising women and men in science who wish to (temporarily) opt out of management positions.<\/li><li>Equal treatment and accommodation: identify best practices on how to avoid undue discrimination based on disability (or measures of positive action) during recruitment and throughout the working life of the disabled staff member.<\/li><li>Better use of diverse abilities towards scientific excellence.<\/li><li>Outreach practices: How to promote the research career amongst underrepresented groups: women and people with disabilities.<\/li><\/ul><h2>2. Scientific career development<\/h2><ul><li>Identify alternative and fulfilling career paths to management in research organisations.<\/li><li>Discuss the criteria for evaluating scientific performance.<\/li><li>Good practices in promoting and valorising from an HR perspective scientific excellence in research.<\/li><\/ul><h2>3. Competency mapping<\/h2><ul><li>Developing a robust competency mapping system: success story sharing<\/li><li>How to make better use of a competency mapping system to support HR forward planning in HR processes such as recruitment planning, learning and development, and mobility, while striving for scientific excellence.<\/li><\/ul><\/div><\/div><\/div>\";s:6:\"format\";s:9:\"full_html\";}}}s:32:\"field_show_latest_block_homepage\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:15:\"field_show_body\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"0\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_subscription_buttons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:22:\"field_background_image\";a:0:{}s:26:\"field_show_welcome_message\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:16:\"field_show_icons\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:31:\"field_show_manager_editor_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_latest_member_block\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:30:\"field_show_last_online_members\";a:1:{s:3:\"und\";a:1:{i:0;a:1:{s:5:\"value\";s:1:\"1\";}}}s:26:\"_drafty_revision_requested\";s:18:\"FIELD_LOAD_CURRENT\";s:11:\"entity_type\";s:4:\"node\";s:11:\"rdf_mapping\";a:9:{s:7:\"rdftype\";a:2:{i:0;s:9:\"sioc:Item\";i:1;s:13:\"foaf:Document\";}s:5:\"title\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:8:\"dc:title\";}}s:7:\"created\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:2:{i:0;s:7:\"dc:date\";i:1;s:10:\"dc:created\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:7:\"changed\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:11:\"dc:modified\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}s:4:\"body\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:15:\"content:encoded\";}}s:3:\"uid\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:has_creator\";}s:4:\"type\";s:3:\"rel\";}s:4:\"name\";a:1:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:9:\"foaf:name\";}}s:13:\"comment_count\";a:2:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:16:\"sioc:num_replies\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:11:\"xsd:integer\";}s:13:\"last_activity\";a:3:{s:10:\"predicates\";a:1:{i:0;s:23:\"sioc:last_activity_date\";}s:8:\"datatype\";s:12:\"xsd:dateTime\";s:8:\"callback\";s:12:\"date_iso8601\";}}s:4:\"p
